      <script language="JavaScript">
       function top_check_log() {
    alert('ログインはSSL対応のログイン画面から行う必要があります。\nログイン画面へ移動します。');
    ssl_login('login', undefined, document.top_form_log.id.value);
}

function MakeShop_TopSearch(e, id) {
    if(e.type == 'keydown' && e.keyCode != 13){
        return;
    }

    if (!document.getElementById(id)) {
        return;
    }

    document.all_view_top.search.value = document.getElementById(id).value;
    document.all_view_top.submit();
}
      </script>
      <script>
       function estimate() {
}
function check_log() {
    alert('ログインはSSL対応のログイン画面から行う必要があります。\nログイン画面へ移動します。');
    ssl_login('login', undefined, document.search.id.value);
}
function CheckKey_log() {
    key=event.keyCode;
    if (key==13) {
        check_log()
    }
}
function CheckKey_search()
{
    key=event.keyCode;
    if (key==13) {
        document.search.submit();
    }
}
function Search(){
    if (document.search.id || document.search.passwd){
        document.search.id.value = '';
        document.search.passwd.value = '';
    }
    document.search.submit();
}
      </script>

          function bottom_privercy() {

         <script type="text/javascript">
          function addTokuPheader() {
        var body = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
        if(body){
	        var frame = document.createElement("iframe");
	        var url = location.href;

	        frame.src = "https://www.makeshop.jp/ssl/pointheader.html?db=sdarts&host=http%253A%252F%252Fwww.s-darts.com";

	        frame.id = "gmo_point_header_iframe";
	        frame.name = "point_header";
	        frame.width = "100%";
	        frame.height = "30";
	        frame.scrolling = "no";
	        frame.border = "0";
	        frame.frameBorder = "0";

	        frame.style.borderBottom = "solid 1px #cccccc";
	        body.insertBefore(frame, body.firstChild);

	        var tNode = document.createTextNode("表示できません");
	        var doc;
	        if (document.all) {
	          // IE
	          doc  = frame.document;
	        } else {
	          // Mozilla
	          doc = frame;
	        }
	        doc.appendChild(tNode);
        }

            }

    function ssoLogin(){
        var scriptTag = document.createElement("script");
        scriptTag.setAttribute("type", "text/javascript");
        scriptTag.setAttribute("src", "https://www.makeshop.jp/api/gmo/is_show_gmo_header.html?callback=isTokuPHeader&db=sdarts");
        document.getElementsByTagName("head").item(0).appendChild(scriptTag);
    }

    function isTokuPHeader(isShowGmoPointHeader, isShowYahooLogo){
        var showGmoPointToolbar = false;
        var useGmoPointExcludingItempost = false;
        var isShowGmoPointMemberSeal = (!isShowGmoPointHeader && !useGmoPointExcludingItempost) ? false : true;
        if(!showGmoPointToolbar){
            // とくPヘッダー表示N なら 常に非表示
            isShowGmoPointHeader = false;
        } else if(!isShowGmoPointHeader && useGmoPointExcludingItempost && showGmoPointToolbar){
            // isShowGmoPointHeaderが false ならとくPヘッダー表示設定でとくPヘッダー制御、とくとくポイント利用設定でとくとくポイント利用制御
            isShowGmoPointHeader = true;
        }

        if(isShowGmoPointHeader || isShowYahooLogo){
        	document.cookie = 'show_tokuP_header' + '=' + '1529819966' + '; path=/;';
            if (window.addEventListener) {
                window.addEventListener("load", addTokuPheader, false);
            }else if (window.attachEvent) {
                window.attachEvent("onload", addTokuPheader);
            }
        } else {
                         // とくPヘッダ非表示設定で、かつオーガニックで、ポイントを利用しない設定以外は block設定
            if(isShowGmoPointMemberSeal){
                // とくPシール表示処理
                var allElements = document.getElementsByTagName("img");
                for (i = 0; i < allElements.length; i++) {
                    if (allElements[i].className == 'tokuP_seal') {
                        allElements[i].style.display = 'block';
                    }
                }

                if(isShowYahooLogo){
                    var allElements = document.getElementsByTagName("img");
                    for (i = 0; i < allElements.length; i++) {
                        if (allElements[i].className == 'back_button_yahoo_shopping') {
                            allElements[i].style.display = 'block';
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
                    }
    }
        ssoLogin();
         </script>

           </div>
          </div>
          <dl class="top_dl01">
           <dt>
            ダーツの楽しさとは？
           </dt>
           <dd>
            <ul>
             <li>
              ダーツは、イギリス発祥の射的スポーツです。日本での一般的なイメージからすると、ダーツがスポーツというのは何だか耳慣れない感じがするかもしれません。
              <br/>
              しかし本場イギリスでは2003年に正式に認定を受けており、また日本でも文科省、厚労省から「教育・競技・生涯スポーツ」の認定を受けています。更には、近年プロ団体の設立やイギリスで開催される世界選手権への出場枠を懸けた大会が開催されたりと、日本においても次第にスポーツとしての認識が浸透してきています。
             </li>
             <li>
              もちろん一方で、ダーツにはレジャー・スポーツとしての側面もあります。
              <br/>
              これは１つにはダーツが、プレイヤーの体力、腕力に拠らないという特性を備えているからです。
             </li>
             <li>
              すなわち、老若男女が同じ土俵で楽しむことが出来るという潜在性の高さを備えた数少ないスポーツだからです。また1つには一般的なスポーツに比べ、必要とされる道具も少ないという気軽さもあります。そして、例えばバスケットボールのフリースローのように、自分が狙ったところにダーツが入るというのは、何とも言えない爽快感があります。
             </li>
             <li>
              また、まったく環境の違う人同士がパブやショップで知り合うきっかけとなったというような、コミュニケ—ションの手段としての面も持ち合わせています。
              <br/>
              ダーツが元来持ち合わせていたこれらのポテンシャルに加え、安全性に優れたソフトダーツ、および専門的な知識を必要としない自動計算機能やICカードによる成績管理機能を実装したマシンの登場により、ソフトダーツの競技人口は急速に拡大しました。
更にソフトダーツから始めた方が、ハードダーツの魅力にも気付き、というようなシナジー効果により、現在ダーツ全体の競技人口は世界中で増え続けています。
             </li>
            </ul>
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </div>
         <!-- 更新情報 -->
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
     </div>

function login_next_page(login_form , parent_location_host , parent_location_pathname , parent_location_search ) {
  type = "login"
  etc = ""
  
  if ( parent_location_host == "item.s-darts.com" ) {
    return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=item:" + parent_location_pathname + parent_location_search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
  } else if ( parent_location_host == "test.item.s-darts.com" ) {
    return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=test:" + parent_location_pathname + parent_location_search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
  } else if ( parent_location_host == "192.168.146.128:3000" ) {
    return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=local:" + parent_location_pathname + parent_location_search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
  } else if ( parent_location_host == "review.s-darts.com" ) {
    return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=review:" + parent_location_pathname + parent_location_search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
  } else {
    return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=www:" + parent_location_pathname + parent_location_search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
  }
  
  login_form.ssl_login_return_url.value = return_url
  login_form.type.value = type;
  login_form.opt.value = etc;
  login_form.submit();
}
 
   function login_check_log(login_form) {
     if (login_form.id){
       old_login_check_log(login_form)
     } else {
       type = "login"
       etc = ""
       
       if ( parent.location.host == "item.s-darts.com" ) {
         return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=item:" + parent.location.pathname + parent.location.search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
       } else if ( parent.location.host == "test.item.s-darts.com" ) {
         return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=test:" + parent.location.pathname + parent.location.search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
       } else if ( parent.location.host == "192.168.146.128:3000" ) {
         return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=local:" + parent.location.pathname + parent.location.search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
       } else if ( parent.location.host == "review.s-darts.com" ) {
         return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=review:" + parent.location.pathname + parent.location.search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
       } else {
         if ( parent.location.host == "www.s-darts.com" &&  parent.location.href.match("&") ) {
           return_url = "/html/page873.html?special_path=www:" + parent.location.pathname + parent.location.search.replace("?",":").replace(/&/g,"||").replace(/=/g,"|")
         } else {
           var tmp = parent.location.href.split("/");
           tmp.splice(0,3);

           return_url = '/' + tmp.join("/");
         }
       }
       
       login_form.ssl_login_return_url.value = return_url
       login_form.type.value = type;
       login_form.opt.value = etc;
       login_form.submit();
     }

   }


 function old_login_check_log(login_form) {
   if (login_form.id.value.length==0) {
     login_form.id.focus();
     alert("会員IDをご入力ください。");return false;
   }
   
   if (login_form.passwd.value.length==0) {
     login_form.passwd.focus();
     alert("パスワードを入力ください。");return false;
   }
   
   var login_page_pathname = parent.location.pathname;
   var login_page_search = parent.location.search;
   var login_page_host = parent.location.host;
   document.cookie = "login_page_pathname=" + login_page_pathname + "; path=/;" + " domain=.s-darts.com;" ;
   document.cookie = "login_page_search=" + login_page_search + "; path=/;" + " domain=.s-darts.com;" ;
   document.cookie = "login_page_host=" + login_page_host + "; path=/;" + " domain=.s-darts.com;" ;

   login_form.submit();
 }

function iframeCreate(url, id, width , height ){
    var target = document.getElementById(id);
    var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
    iframe.frameBorder = '0';
    iframe.scrolling = 'no';
    iframe.width = width ;
    iframe.height = height ;
    iframe.src = url;
    
    target.appendChild(iframe);
    
    // IE・Chrome対応
    iframe.contentWindow.location.href = iframe.src;
}

function footerCalenderDisplay(){
    $("#footer_calender").html("");
    iframeCreate("http://gigaplus.makeshop.jp/sdarts/calender/index.html" , "footer_calender" , 251 , 220 ) ;
}

setTimeout("footerCalenderDisplay()", 3000 ) ;
})

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function drawChart(draw_id,percentage,slice_color,bg_color) {
        $("#percentage_area").html(percentage+"%")
        $("#mod_percentage").html(( 100 - percentage )+"%")

        var percentage_str = ""
        percentage_str = percentage + "," + ( 100 - percentage )
        
        html_string  = ''
        html_string += '<img src="http://chart.googleapis.com/chart?cht=p&chd=t:'
        html_string += percentage_str
        html_string += '&chs=200x200&chco=' + slice_color + '|ffffff&chp=4.712&amp;chf=bg,s,' + bg_color + '" '
        html_string += 'style="width: 196px;height: 196px;margin: -8px 0px 0px -8px;">'
        $("#"+draw_id).html(html_string)

      }

      function drawIconChart(draw_id,percentage,slice_color,bg_color) {
        if ( percentage == 0 ) {
          $("#percentage_area2").html('<font color="#444">メール便</font><br>0%')
        }else{
          $("#percentage_area2").html('<font color="#444">メール便</font><br>' + percentage +  '%')
        }
        
        percentage_str = ""
        
        if ( percentage > 100 ){
          $("#percentage_area2").hide()
          $("#percentage_area2_arrow").hide()
          $("#percentage_area3").show()
          $(".right_area_pospacket").addClass("pospacket_ng")
          percentage_str = "0,100"
        } else {
          $("#percentage_area3").hide()
          $("#percentage_area2").show()
          $("#percentage_area2_arrow").show()
          $(".right_area_pospacket").removeClass("pospacket_ng")
          percentage_str = percentage + "," + ( 100 - percentage )
        
        }
        
        html_string  = ''
        html_string += '<img src="http://chart.googleapis.com/chart?cht=p&chd=t:'
        html_string += percentage_str
        html_string += '&chs=200x200&chco=' + slice_color + '|ffffff&chp=4.712&amp;chf=bg,s,' + bg_color + '" '
        html_string += 'style="width: 42px;height: 42px;margin: -2px -8px;padding: 0;">'
        $("#"+draw_id).html(html_string)
        
      }
      
      function getCartMoreHtmlString(){
        var cart_item_parts_html = ""
        cart_item_parts_html += '  <td colspan=3 class="more_link_area">'
        cart_item_parts_html += '    <a href="http://www.s-darts.com/shop/basket.html"><img src="/images/cart_more.png"></a>'
        cart_item_parts_html += '  </td>'
        
        return cart_item_parts_html
      }
      function getCartItemHtmlString(cart_item,first_column_flg){
        var cart_item_parts_html = ""
        if ( cart_item ){
          cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headImg">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '    <a href="http://www.s-darts.com/shopdetail/' + cart_item["item_system_id"] + '/">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '      <img border="0" src="http://www.s-darts.com/shopimages/sdarts/' + cart_item["item_system_id"] + '5.jpg">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '    </a></td>'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  </td>'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headItem">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '    <a href="http://www.s-darts.com/shopdetail/' + cart_item["item_system_id"] + '/">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '      <span class="item_area">'
          
          if ( cart_item["maker_name"] == "" ){
            cart_item_parts_html += '        <span class="item_name">' + cart_item["goods_name"] +  '</span>'
          } else {
            cart_item_parts_html += '        <span class="maker_name">' + cart_item["maker_name"] +  '</span><br>'
            cart_item_parts_html += '        <span class="goods_name">' + cart_item["goods_name"] +  '</span>'
          }
          
          cart_item_parts_html += '      </span>'
          cart_item_parts_html += '    </a>'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  </td>'
          if ( first_column_flg ){
            cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headNum first_column">'
          } else {
            cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headNum">'
          }
          cart_item_parts_html += '    ' + cart_item["amount"] + '点'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  </td>'
        } else {
          cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headImg">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  </td>'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headItem">'
          cart_item_parts_html += '  </td>'
          if ( first_column_flg ){
            cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headNum first_column"></td>'
          } else {
            cart_item_parts_html += '  <td class="M_headNum"></td>'
          }
        }
        return cart_item_parts_html

      }

       var recieve_cart_info = {};
       function SDarts_toggleCartInfo(opened_flg ){
         if ( opened_flg ) {
           if ( ! $(".right_basketMarginBox tbody tr").get(0) ){
             cartItemShow(recieve_cart_info)
           }
           $(".right_basketMarginBox").show()
         } else {
           $(".right_basketMarginBox").hide()
         }
       }



       function pospaketInfoOpen(){
           cartInfoClose()
           if ( ! $(".right_area_pospacket_info .right_basketMarginBox tbody tr").get(0) ){
             pospaketInfoShow()
           }
           $(".right_area_pospacket_info .right_basketMarginBox").show()
       }
       function pospaketInfoClose(){
         $(".right_area_pospacket_info .right_basketMarginBox").hide()
       }

       function cartInfoOpen(){
           pospaketInfoClose()
           if ( ! $(".right_area_cart_item .right_basketMarginBox tbody tr").get(0) ){
             cartItemShow(recieve_cart_info)
           }
           $(".right_area_cart_item .right_basketMarginBox").show()
       }
       function cartInfoClose(){
         $(".right_area_cart_item .right_basketMarginBox").hide()
       }

       function addFigure(str) {
         var num = new String(str).replace(/,/g, "");
         while(num != (num = num.replace(/^(-?\d+)(\d{3})/, "$1,$2")));
         return num;
       }


      function pospaketInfoShow(){
        html_string = ""
        html_string += "<tr>"
        html_string += "<td>"
        


        if ( ! $("#percentage_area3").is(":hidden") ){
          html_string += '  <div class="pospacket_ng_msg_wrap pospacket_msg_wrap"> '
          html_string += '    <div class="pospacket_ng_msg01" > '
          html_string += '        <p class="pospacket_ng_msg0101" > '

          if ( pospacket_info["max_money_ng"] ) {
            html_string += '    メール便でお届けできる<span>金額</span>を<br>'
            html_string += '    超えています'
          } else if ( pospacket_info["height_ng"] ) {
            html_string += '    カートにメール便対象外商品が<br>'
            html_string += '    含まれています'
          } else if ( pospacket_info["total_fill_percent"] > 100 || ( pospacket_info["height_limit"] && pospacket_info["height_limit_ng"] ) ){
            html_string += '    メール便でお届けできる容量を<br>'
            html_string += '    超えています'
          }
          html_string += '        </p> '

          html_string += '  <p class="pospacket_ng_msg0102" >'
          html_string += '    この注文は'
          html_string += '    <span class="pospacket_ng_msg010201">「ヤマト宅急便」</span>で<br> '
          if ( pospacket_info["max_money_ng"] ) {
            html_string += '<span class="pospacket_ng_msg010202" >送料無料で</span>'
          }
          html_string += 'お送りいたします</p> '
          
          
          html_string += '  <p class="pospacket_msg0103"> '
          html_string += '    <a href="http://www.s-darts.com/html/page898.html" target="_blank"><span>メール便とは？</span></a> '
          html_string += '  </p> '
          html_string += '      </div></div> '

        } else {


          if ( pospacket_info["height_limit"] && ( pospacket_info["total_fill_percent"] < 100 ) ){
            html_string += '  <div class="pospacket_msg_ok_wrap pospacket_msg_wrap height_limit" > '
          } else {
            html_string += '  <div class="pospacket_msg_ok_wrap pospacket_msg_wrap" > '
          }
          html_string += '    <p class="pospacket_ok_msg01">メール便容量</p> '
          html_string += '    <div id="pacman" ></div> '
          html_string += '    <span class="pospacket_ok_msg02" id="percentage_area">' + pospacket_info["total_fill_percent"] + '%</span> '
          html_string += '    <span class="pospacket_ok_msg05" ></span> '
          html_string += '    <p class="pospacket_ok_msg03" >あと<span id="mod_percentage" >%</span>分発送できます</p> '

          if ( pospacket_info["height_limit"] && ( pospacket_info["total_fill_percent"] < 100 ) ){
            html_string += '    <div class="pospacket_ok_msg04" > '
            html_string += '      メール便でお送りできる大きさは、34cm×25cm（A4サイズ大）以内、厚さ3.5cm以内です。 <br> '
            html_string += '      <br> '
            html_string += '      「雑誌」は34cm×25cm、厚さ1〜1.5cmのため、厚みが2cmを超える商品をメール便で一緒に送ることができません。 <br> '
            html_string += '      <br> '
            html_string += '      そのため【 メール便容量 】が100%未満の場合でも'
            html_string += '      「雑誌」と厚みが2cmを超える商品をご一緒にご購入していただく場合は「ヤマト宅急便」で発送させていただきます。<br> '
            html_string += '    </div> '
          }
          html_string += '    <p class="pospacket_msg0103"> '
          html_string += '      <a href="http://www.s-darts.com/html/page898.html" target="_blank"><span>メール便とは？</span></a> '
          html_string += '    </p> '
          html_string += '  </div> '

        }
        html_string += "</td>"
        html_string += "</tr>"
        $(".right_area_pospacket_info .right_basketMarginBox tbody").html(html_string)
        if ( $("#percentage_area3").is(":hidden") ){
          drawChart('pacman', pospacket_info["total_fill_percent"],'007ebb',"ffffff")
        }
      }


      function cartItemShow(in_cart_info){
         var cart_item_html = ""
         var cart_item_record_count = 5
         
         if ( in_cart_info["cart_item"].length < cart_item_record_count ){
           cart_item_record_count = in_cart_info["cart_item"].length 
         }
         
         var first_column_flg = true
         for ( i = 0 ; i < cart_item_record_count + 1 ; i++ ){
           if ( i == 0 ) {
             cart_item_html += '<tr >'
             if ( in_cart_info["cart_item"].length > cart_item_record_count ){
               first_column_flg = true
               cart_item_html += getCartItemHtmlString(in_cart_info["cart_item"][cart_item_record_count],first_column_flg)
             }
             cart_item_html += '  <th colspan=3 class="order_info">'
             cart_item_html += '  注文合計金額　<span id="total_money">' + addFigure(in_cart_info["total_money"]) +  '</span>円<br>'
             
             //cart_item_html += '  12/26 16時まで 全品送料無料'
             if ( in_cart_info["mod_money_for_delivery_free"] == 0 ) {
               cart_item_html += '  送料無料'
             } else {
               cart_item_html += '  あと'+ addFigure(in_cart_info["mod_money_for_delivery_free"]) +'円で送料無料'
             }
             cart_item_html += '  </th>'
             
             cart_item_html += '</tr>'
           } else {
             if ( i == cart_item_record_count ) {
               cart_item_html += '<tr class="last-child">'
             } else {
               cart_item_html += '<tr>'
             }
             
             first_column_flg = true
             
             if ( in_cart_info["cart_item"].length > cart_item_record_count ){
               if ( i == cart_item_record_count && in_cart_info["cart_item"][cart_item_record_count + i + 1 ] ) {
                 cart_item_html += getCartMoreHtmlString(null, first_column_flg)
               } else {
                 cart_item_html += getCartItemHtmlString(in_cart_info["cart_item"][cart_item_record_count + i], first_column_flg)
               }
             }
             first_column_flg = false
             cart_item_html += getCartItemHtmlString(in_cart_info["cart_item"][i-1] , first_column_flg)
             cart_item_html += '</tr>'
           }
         }
         if ( in_cart_info["cart_item"].length > cart_item_record_count ){
           $(".right_area_cart_item .right_basketMarginBox table").addClass("two_column")
         }
         $(".right_area_cart_item .right_basketMarginBox tbody").html(cart_item_html)
      }

      var pospacket_info = null

      function onMessage(messageEvent) {  
         if ( messageEvent.origin != "http://www.s-darts.com" ){
           return
         }
         
         if ( messageEvent.data["action"] == "cart_update" ) {
           cartInfoUpdate()
           return
         }

         if ( messageEvent.data["cart_info"]["cart_count"] == 0 ) {
           $("#cart_count").html("0")
         } else {
           $("#cart_count").html(messageEvent.data["cart_info"]["cart_count"])
         }

         pospacket_info = messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]

           $("#main").removeClass("pospacket_height_limit_wrap")
           
           if ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["total_fill_percent"] > 100 ) {
             drawIconChart('pacman2', 121,'007ebb',"00aed9")
           } else {
             if ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["max_money_ng"] ) {
               drawIconChart('pacman2', 123,'007ebb',"00aed9")
             } else if ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["height_ng"] ) {
               drawIconChart('pacman2', 124,'007ebb',"00aed9")
             } else if ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["height_limit"] && messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["height_limit_ng"] ) {
               drawIconChart('pacman2', 125,'007ebb',"00aed9")
             } else if ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["total_fill_percent"] > 100 ) {
               drawIconChart('pacman2', 126,'007ebb',"00aed9")
             } else {
               if ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["height_limit"] && ( messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["total_fill_percent"] < 100 )  ){
                 $("#main").addClass("pospacket_height_limit_wrap")
               }
               drawIconChart('pacman2', messageEvent.data["pospacket_info"]["total_fill_percent"] ,'007ebb',"00aed9")
             }
           }

         recieve_cart_info = messageEvent.data["cart_info"]
         $(".right_basketMarginBox tbody").html("")
         $("#right_area").show()
         
      }

function orderDisplyNone( tr_elms1 , i , inner_html_str ) {
  if ( tr_elms1.length > i ) {
    var td_elms1 = tr_elms1[i].getElementsByTagName("td");
    // console.log( tr_elms1[i].innerHTML )
    if ( td_elms1.length > 0 ) {
      var b_elms1 = td_elms1[0].getElementsByTagName("b");
      if ( b_elms1.length > 0 ) {
        if ( b_elms1[0].innerHTML == inner_html_str ) {
          tr_elms1[i].style.display = "none"
          td_elms1[0].style.display = "none"
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

function makeshopCookieWrite( cookie_key , cookie_value){
  document.cookie = cookie_key + "=" + cookie_value + ";path=/"  +   "; domain=www.makeshop.jp;" 
}

function pre_send(){
  makeshopCookieWrite( "sdarts_basket_deliverly_method" , "still")

  if ( jQuery('#deli_ymd option:selected').get(0) && jQuery('#deli_ymd option:selected').val() != "__" ) {
    makeshopCookieWrite( "sdarts_basket_deliverly_method" , "youpack")
  }

  if ( jQuery('select[name="deli_time"] option:selected').get(0) && jQuery('select[name="deli_time"] option:selected').val() != "指定なし" ) {
    makeshopCookieWrite( "sdarts_basket_deliverly_method" , "youpack")
  }
  
  send()
}

function is_mobile_main() {
  var useragents = [
    'iPhone',         // Apple iPhone
    'iPod',           // Apple iPod touch
    'Android',        // 1.5+ Android
    'dream',          // Pre 1.5 Android
    'CUPCAKE',        // 1.5+ Android
    'blackberry9500', // Storm
    'blackberry9530', // Storm
    'blackberry9520', // Storm v2
    'blackberry9550', // Storm v2
    'blackberry9800', // Torch
    'webOS',          // Palm Pre Experimental
    'incognito',      // Other iPhone browser
    'webmate'         // Other iPhone browser
  ];
  
  var pc_useragents = [
    'Nexus 7',         // Nexus 7
    'Nexus 10'         // Nexus 10
  ];
  
  var pattern = new RegExp(useragents.join('|'), 'i');
  var pattern2 = new RegExp(pc_useragents.join('|'), 'i');
  
  if (pattern2.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
    return false;
  } else {
    return pattern.test(navigator.userAgent) ;
  }
}

function deliverlrHopeDateSet(){
  var reservation = 0;
  var reservation_codes = "";
  
  alltables = document.getElementsByTagName("table")
  for (i1 = 0; i1 < alltables.length; i1++) {
    if ( alltables[i1].className == "responsiveDesignBasket" ) {
      tds = alltables[i1].getElementsByTagName("td");
      for (i2 = 0; i2 < tds.length; i2++) {
        if ( jQuery(tds[i2]).html().match(/予約商品/)  ){
          if ( jQuery(tds[i2]).find("a").get(0) ) {
            reservation_codes = reservation_codes + "|" + jQuery(tds[i2]).find("a").attr("href").replace("http://www.s-darts.com/shopdetail/","")
            reservation = 1
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }

  if (jQuery('#receiver_user_type_X').is(":checked")) {

    pref_name = jQuery("select[name='sender_area'] option:selected").html().replace(/(^\s+)|(\s+$)/g, "")
    address = jQuery("input[name='sender_addr']").val()
  } else {
    pref_code = jQuery("select[name='area']").val();
    pref_name = jQuery("select[name='area'] option:selected").html().replace(/(^\s+)|(\s+$)/g, "")
    address = jQuery("input[name='address']").val()
  }

  ajax_url = "https://global.s-darts.com/checkout/change_pref.js"
  var sdarts_login_id = GetCookie("sdarts_login_id")

  query = ""
  jQuery("table.responsiveDesignBasket > tbody > tr").each(function(){
    if ( ! jQuery(this).hasClass("responsiveDesignBasketHeader") ){
      if ( jQuery(this).find("td:nth-child(1) > a").get(0) ){
        item_system_id = jQuery(this).find("td:nth-child(1) > a").attr("href").replace("http://www.s-darts.com/shopdetail/" , "")
        amount = jQuery(this).find("td:nth-child(2)").html().replace(/\s/g , "")
        query += "|" + item_system_id + "," + amount;
      }
    }
  })

  query = query.substring(1,99999) ;


//  if ( sdarts_login_id == "" ){

//  }
  
  if ( pref_code != "0" && address != "" ) {

    var tmp_deli_ymd = jQuery('#deli_ymd option:selected').val();

    document.getElementById("deli_month").value = deli_ymd[1];
    document.getElementById("deli_day").value = deli_ymd[2];

    
    
    post_data = { 
      "pref_name" : pref_name ,
      "address" : address ,
      "uid" : sdarts_login_id,
      "query" : query
    }

    if ( reservation == 1 ) {
      jQuery(function(){
        post_data["reservation_codes"] = escape(reservation_codes.substring(1,99999))

        jQuery.ajax({
          url: ajax_url,
          data: post_data,
          dataType: "script",
          type:"post"
        });
      })
    } else {
      jQuery(function(){

        jQuery.ajax({
          url: ajax_url,
          data: post_data,
          dataType: "script",
          type:"post"
        });
      })
    
    }
  } else {
    post_data = { 
      "uid" : sdarts_login_id,
      "query" : query
    }

    
    jQuery.ajax({
      url: ajax_url,
      data: post_data,
      dataType: "script",
      type:"post"
    });

    default_postal_code = ""

      check_postal = jQuery("#sender_post1").val() + jQuery("#sender_post2").val() 
      if ( default_postal_code != check_postal ) {
        deliverlrHopeDateSet()
      }
    })
    
    jQuery("input[name='addr']").blur(function(){
      check_postal = jQuery("#receiver_post1").val() + jQuery("#receiver_post2").val() 
      if ( default_postal_code != check_postal ) {

      }
    })
  }
}

function GetCookie(name) {
	var regexp = new RegExp('; ' + name + '(=([^;]*))?;'); 
	var cookies = document.cookie
	var match  = ('; ' + document.cookie + ';').match(regexp);
	if (match) {
		ord = match[2];
	}
	else {
		ord = "";
	}
	return ord;
}

function script_require( uri ) {
  var script  = document.createElement( 'script' );
  script.type = 'text/javascript';
  script.src  = uri;
  var body    = document.getElementsByTagName( 'body' )[0];
  body.appendChild( script );
}

  function smartphoneAddScript(url){
    var el = document.createElement("script");
    el.setAttribute("src",url);
    el.setAttribute("charset","UTF-8");
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(el);
  }

  function smartphoneAddScriptEuc(url){
    var el = document.createElement("script");
    el.setAttribute("src",url);
    el.setAttribute("charset","EUC-JP");
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(el);
  }

  function smartphoneAddStyle(url){
    var el = document.createElement("link");
    el.setAttribute("href",url);
    el.setAttribute("type","text/css");
    el.setAttribute("rel","stylesheet");
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(el);
  }

function forgotLinkModify(){

      a_elms1[0].innerHTML = "&gt;&gt;&nbsp;ID/パスワードを忘れた方はこちら"
    }
  }
}

  if ( location.pathname == "/ssl/smartphone/login.html" ) {
    if( window.addEventListener )
    {
        window.addEventListener( 'load', forgotLinkModify , false );
    }
    else if( window.attachEvent )
    {
        window.attachEvent( 'onload', forgotLinkModify );
    }
    else
    {
        window.onload=forgotLinkModify
    }
  }

  <script language="JavaScript">
   function ssl_login(type, etc, user_id){
        var etc = (typeof(etc) != "undefined") ? etc : '';
        var user_id = (typeof(user_id) != "undefined") ? user_id : '';
        var msg_index = {
            "member" : "登録済みの会員情報を変更するにはログインが必要です。\nログイン画面へ移動します。\n会員登録は、ログイン画面から会員登録画面へ移動してください。",
            "reserve" : "ポイント照会にはログインが必要です。\nログイン画面へ移動します。",
            "confirm" : "注文履歴にはログイン、または注文番号が必要です。\nログイン画面へ移動します。"
        };

        if (type == 'no_reserve') {
            alert('ポイント機能はご利用いただけません');
            return;
        }
        if(typeof(msg_index[type]) != "undefined"){
            alert(msg_index[type]);
        }
        if (typeof(ga) === 'function') { ga('linker:decorate', document.ssl_login_form); }

        // 上段 + メインフレームタイプの場合return_url
        if(typeof(parent.main) != "undefined" && typeof(parent.main.location) != "undefined"){
            var rtn_url = 0;
            var tmp = parent.main.location.href.split("/");
            tmp.splice(0,3);

            if(/^[main][a-z0-9]+\.html/.test(tmp[1])){
                rtn_url = 1;
            }else if(tmp[0] == 'shopdetail'){
                rtn_url = 1;
            }else if(tmp[0] == 'shopbrand'){
                rtn_url = 1;
            }else if(tmp[1] == 'basket.html'){
                rtn_url = 1;
            }

            if(rtn_url == 1){
                document.ssl_login_form.ssl_login_return_url.value = '/' + tmp.join("/");
            }
        }
        if(type == 'amazon_basket_login') {
    document.ssl_login_form.amazon_login_type.value = type;
    document.ssl_login_form.action = 'https://www.makeshop.jp/ssl/amazon/amazon_login.html?db=sdarts';
    type = 'qmember';
}

        document.ssl_login_form.type.value = type;
        document.ssl_login_form.opt.value = etc;
        document.ssl_login_form.user_id.value = user_id;
        document.ssl_login_form.submit();
    }
